Fantastic, honest professional!  My 46 year old Seiko watch had stopped working, and I had Fred do a cleaning, at a very reasonable price, as other repair shops refused to merely clean it, insisting I needed an outrageously priced overhaul. I can heartily recommend Fred, a very personable and honest individual who takes pride in his profession, and does excellent work.</Text>

<userid>109398224756512229136<//userid>< Name>
Brian Weiss< /Name>
<date>1496230680854< /date><Rate>4< /Rate>< text>
The Ritter Center is a non profit organization that ostensibley serves the low income, and homeless population of Marin County and environs with a food pantry, day services; showers, needed clothing, and the  medical arts; physical and mental health. They also have a staff of advocates who are knowledgeable in community and other resources such as jobs and housing and particulars. Ritter has been a bedrock of the community for over 40 years, and continues to do, what can be described as, the daily nitty gritty of human services. They are a hearty group, and seemingly dedicated to their mission . Of course, my understanding of them is subjective, and by no means do I represent them. More can be learned by visiting their website, which readers must get for themselves.<//text>

<review>This is a difficult review to put to paper. I ordered a Blackbird, paid for it, and took delivery 9 months later. The delays were out of the control of Bolton Ebikes. I understand that. The bike quality is very (very) high, and the price is amazing for the quality received. However... customer service is unsatisfactory for a modern company. They have a policy of scheduled phone calls only. It was a week away to the first available call-slot when I had difficulty assembling my new bike. Their primary way to communicate is via email. This meant that when I ran into a problem putting my bike together, I had to stop, write an email and wait (until the next day). Their answer was helpful, but did NOT fix the problem.
When you prepay for a $2,500.00 bike and wait months for it to arrive, you should expect a more timely response to customer communications. I am sure Kyle has a host of reasons why they do not have phone based customer service, but from the customer point-of-view, his reasons do not matter. I can confirm Bolton received our email regarding our concerns. As an IT company, we utilize an appliance that intercepts, records,  and monitors ALL email communications sent and received. Kyle's YouTube videos brought me to BOLTON EBIKES.  I'm 71 years old and wanted Transportation that I could hang on a rack behind my Jeep or motor home. I drove to their shop and test drove one of the FoxBat 1,000 watt models. Kyle and the guys were extremely helpful and informative. I bought the E-bike and several options to make the bike comfortable for me. The components used are much better than E-bikes costing much more. I'll post again once I know how the service is. Michael

Okay, I said I'd do a follow-up once I  knew more about Bolton Ebikes from a service perspective. I had the Foxbat for a couple of weeks and tried various changes in handlebar position and seat positions. Nothing worked for me to ride for more than a couple of miles. I'm a big guy and the rider position put all my upper body mass squarely on my wrists and that was painful!
Kyle at Bolton Ebikes invited me to try the Cheetah cruiser style ebike.  I rode it a little over 2 miles around their shop and was completely sold on the Cheetah! Kyle gave me a full refund towards the purchase of the Cheetah after I had offered $500 deduction because I had ridden the Foxbat for a couple of weeks (I believed that to be fair). So, Bolton Ebikes showed me that customer satisfaction is VERY IMPORTANT to them.
By the way, the very next day I took the Cheetah for a 10 mile enjoyable ride. I wouldn't recommend any place other than Bolton Ebikes for you ebike purchase.
Great products, great prices, and great service!

By the way, for other senior citizens, the Cheetah is the best ebike on the planet. Order one, ride one, and you'll be very pleased that you did!

Michael< /Review>
